# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`

# Task: Implement Custom Header Injection Filter for Envoy

## Objective
Create a new HTTP filter `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection` that injects
configurable headers into requests and/or responses based on route metadata.

## Requirements

1. **Create filter source files**:
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h` — filter class declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc` — filter implementation
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h` — factory declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc` — factory registration

2. **Filter behavior**:
   - Implements `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` (request path) and `Http::StreamEncoderFilter` (response path)
   - Reads header injection rules from filter config
   - Supports both request and response header injection
   - Follows Envoy's filter lifecycle (decodeHeaders, encodeHeaders)

3. **Create test file**:
   - `test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter_test.cc`

## Key Reference Files
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.h` — simple header filter pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.cc` — implementation pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/config.cc` — factory registration
- `source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h` — factory base class

## Success Criteria
- Filter header file declares class inheriting from StreamDecoderFilter/StreamEncoderFilter
- Filter implementation has decodeHeaders/encodeHeaders methods
- Factory config file registers the filter
- Follows Envoy naming: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection
- Test file exists

     1→#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"
     2→
     3→#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"
     4→
     5→#include "source/common/http/header_utility.h"
     6→#include "source/common/http/utility.h"
     7→
     8→namespace Envoy {
     9→namespace Extensions {
    10→namespace HttpFilters {
    11→namespace CustomHeaderInjection {
    12→
    13→Config::Config(const ProtoConfig& proto_config, const bool per_route) {
    14→  // Process request rules
    15→  for (const auto& rule : proto_config.request_rules()) {
    16→    request_rules_.push_back(rule);
    17→  }
    18→
    19→  // Process response rules
    20→  for (const auto& rule : proto_config.response_rules()) {
    21→    response_rules_.push_back(rule);
    22→  }
    23→
    24→  // Note: empty configs are fine for the global config, which would be the case for enabling
    25→  // the filter globally without rules and then applying them at the virtual host or
    26→  // route level. At the virtual or route level, it makes no sense to have an empty
    27→  // config so we throw an error.
    28→  if (per_route && request_rules_.empty() && response_rules_.empty()) {
    29→    throw EnvoyException("custom_header_injection_filter: Per filter configs must at least specify "
    30→                         "either request or response rules");
    31→  }
    32→}
    33→
    34→CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(const ConfigSharedPtr config)
    35→    : config_(config) {}
    36→
    37→CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::~CustomHeaderInjectionFilter() = default;
    38→

### Key Features:

✅ **Filter Implementation**
- Inherits from `Http::StreamFilter` (both decoder and encoder)
- Implements `decodeHeaders()` for request header injection
- Implements `encodeHeaders()` for response header injection
- Properly handles data and trailer pass-through

✅ **Configuration**
- Reads header injection rules from filter config
- Supports both request and response rules
- Implements per-route configuration override support
- Validates per-route configs (must have at least one rule)

✅ **Factory Pattern**
- Registers with name `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection`
- Implements `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` interface
- Creates filter instances via factory callbacks

✅ **Test Coverage**

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

using ProtoConfig = envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjection;
using HeaderInjectionRule = envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::HeaderInjectionRule;

/**
 * Configuration for the custom header injection filter.
 */
class Config : public ::Envoy::Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig,
               public Logger::Loggable<Logger::Id::config> {
public:
  Config(const ProtoConfig& proto_config, bool per_route = false);

  const std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule>& requestRules() const { return request_rules_; }
  const std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule>& responseRules() const { return response_rules_; }
  bool hasRequestRules() const { return !request_rules_.empty(); }
  bool hasResponseRules() const { return !response_rules_.empty(); }

private:
  std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule> request_rules_;
  std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule> response_rules_;
};

using ConfigSharedPtr = std::shared_ptr<Config>;

/**
 * Custom Header Injection filter that injects configurable headers into
 * requests and/or responses.
 */

                                    public Logger::Loggable<Logger::Id::filter> {
public:
  CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(const ConfigSharedPtr config);
  ~CustomHeaderInjectionFilter() override;

  void onDestroy() override {}

2. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"

#include "source/common/http/header_utility.h"
#include "source/common/http/utility.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

Config::Config(const ProtoConfig& proto_config, const bool per_route) {
  // Process request rules
  for (const auto& rule : proto_config.request_rules()) {
    request_rules_.push_back(rule);
  }

  // Process response rules
  for (const auto& rule : proto_config.response_rules()) {
    response_rules_.push_back(rule);
  }

  // Note: empty configs are fine for the global config, which would be the case for enabling
  // the filter globally without rules and then applying them at the virtual host or
  // route level. At the virtual or route level, it makes no sense to have an empty
  // config so we throw an error.
  if (per_route && request_rules_.empty() && response_rules_.empty()) {
    throw EnvoyException("custom_header_injection_filter: Per filter configs must at least specify "
                         "either request or response rules");
  }
}

CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(const ConfigSharedPtr config)
    : config_(config) {}

CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::~CustomHeaderInjectionFilter() = default;

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,
                                                                     bool) {
  const auto* config = getConfig();
  if (config->hasRequestRules()) {
    injectHeaders(headers, config->requestRules());
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

Http::FilterFactoryCb CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjection&
        proto_config,
    const std::string&, Server::Configuration::FactoryContext&) {
  ConfigSharedPtr filter_config(std::make_shared<Config>(proto_config));

  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {
    callbacks.addStreamFilter(
        Http::StreamFilterSharedPtr{new CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(filter_config)});
  };
}

absl::StatusOr<Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfigConstSharedPtr>
CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjection&
        config,
    Server::Configuration::ServerFactoryContext&, ProtobufMessage::ValidationVisitor&) {
  return std::make_shared<const Config>(config, true);
}

/**
 * Static registration for the custom header injection filter.
 * @see RegisterFactory.
 */
REGISTER_FACTORY(CustomHeaderInjectionConfig, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory);

} // namespace CustomHeaderInjection
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy

package envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3;

import "udpa/annotations/status.proto";
import "validate/validate.proto";

option java_package = "io.envoyproxy.envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3";
option java_outer_classname = "CustomHeaderInjectionProto";
option java_multiple_files = true;
option go_package = "github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3;custom_header_injectionv3";
option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = ACTIVE;

// [#protodoc-title: Custom Header Injection Filter]
//
// The configuration for injecting custom headers into requests and responses.
//
// Custom Header Injection :ref:`configuration overview <config_http_filters_custom_header_injection>`.
// [#extension: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection]

message CustomHeaderInjection {
  // Request header injection rules.
  repeated HeaderInjectionRule request_rules = 1;

  // Response header injection rules.
  repeated HeaderInjectionRule response_rules = 2;
}

message HeaderInjectionRule {
  // The name of the header to inject.
  string header_name = 1 [(validate.rules).string = {min_len: 1}];

  // The value of the header to inject.
  string header_value = 2;
}

10. WRITE /workspace/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md
# Custom Header Injection Filter Implementation

## Overview
This implementation provides a new HTTP filter `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection` for Envoy that injects configurable headers into requests and/or responses.

## Files Created

### Source Files
1. **source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h**
   - Declares `CustomHeaderInjectionFilter` class inheriting from `Http::StreamFilter`
   - Declares `Config` class for filter configuration
   - Implements both `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` and `Http::StreamEncoderFilter` interfaces
   - Key methods: `decodeHeaders()`, `encodeHeaders()`, `injectHeaders()`

2. **source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc**
   - Implements filter class and configuration logic
   - `Config` constructor parses request and response injection rules
   - `decodeHeaders()` injects headers into requests
   - `encodeHeaders()` injects headers into responses
   - Supports per-route configuration overrides
   - Implements header injection logic via `injectHeaders()` method

3. **source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h**
   - Declares `CustomHeaderInjectionConfig` factory class
   - Inherits from `Common::FactoryBase<ProtoConfig>`
   - Registers with name "envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection"

4. **source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc**
   - Implements factory methods:
     - `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` - creates filter instances
     - `createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped()` - creates per-route configs
   - Registers factory with Envoy's NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory

### Proto Definition
5. **api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.proto**
   - Defines `CustomHeaderInjection` message
